gitea as git server
i heavily use git all the time thus years ago i already replaced gitlab with gitea – a lightweight painless self hosted git servic gitea itself is a fork of gogs which was not really c these days gitea is a way more active and prospering project than as reverse proxy in mailu
so how do you “attach” gitea to a running mailu infrastructure  mailu itself 
adding gitea entry to nginx override
having said that to add gitea to nginx create this file datamailuoverrideconf

location gitea 
  proxy pass httpgit3000

and that’s i
additional entry to docker compose
to start gitea itself add it to mailu’s docker composeyml

   gitea

  git
    image giteagitealatest
    restart always
    env file mailu254
    volumes
        datagiteadata
        etctimezoneetctimezonero
       2222
note the shared volumes that way the gitea configuration file will be written on your storage in datagiteagiteaconfapp
also we want to set uid and guid for gitea via environment variablesenv


 gitea settings

user uid1000
user gid1000
